dub,duc,dud,due,duj,dtr=duh(dty:sub(1,2),16),duh(dty:sub(3,4),16),duh(dty:sub(5,6),16),duh(dty:sub(7,8),16),duh(dty:sub(9,10),16),{}for duk=0,duj-1 do dtr[dty:sub(11+duk,11+duk)]=duk end local dts,dtw,dtx,kk,gi,dtz="",{},0,dub,0,95 while dtz<#dty do local lo=dtr[dty:sub(dtz,dtz)]or 0 local hi=dtr[dty:sub(dtz+1,dtz+1)]or 0 local dum=lo+hi*duj dtx=dtx+1;dtw[dtx]=dtu(dtv(dtv(dum,dud),kk)%256)kk=(kk*duc+gi+due)%256;gi=gi+1;dtz=dtz+2 if dtx>=256 then dts=dts..duf(dtw);dtw={};dtx=0 end end if dtx>0 then dts=dts..duf(dtw)end local dul,dun=nil,160 if dun==160 then local a,b=(loadstring or load)(dts);if a then dul=a else warn("[PVM] "..tostring(b))end;dun=157 end local duo if dun==157 then if dul then duo=dul end;dun=162 end if dun==162 and duo then return duo(...)end end)()
